+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+Requires-Dist: PyYAML>=6.0.2
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+- [docs/junit_parser_contract.md](docs/junit_parser_contract.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--enrich-github` | disabled | Enable optional GitHub issue/PR metadata enrichment |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--github-token TOKEN` | `$(GITHUB_TOKEN)` | Token used for GitHub API calls |
+| `--github-enrichment-cache PATH` | `<out>/github_enrichment_cache.json` | Optional local cache for enrichment responses |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### Command artifact contract (current scaffold)
+
+For `--out` directory `./out`, the scaffold writes command-specific artifacts:
+
+- `manifest.json`
+  - command metadata and step status for each run invocation
+- `events.jsonl`
+  - machine-readable execution events for the same run
+- `repo_profile.json`, `scan.jsonl`, `candidates.jsonl` for `mine`
+- `reviewed.jsonl`, `review.md`, `review.html` for `review`
+- `materialized.jsonl`, `materialization_rejections.jsonl`, `dataset/dataset.jsonl`,
+  `dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl`, `adapter_<repo>.py`, `specs.json` for `export`
+- `validation.jsonl` for `eval`
+
+This list reflects what the v0.1 scaffold guarantees today; future stages
+extend it to include run-level and analysis artifacts.
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

LLM Judgemuch worse
Overall Δ
-1.80
Confidence
0.92

Candidate partially carries usage/cost provenance through runtime results, but misses key schema and failure-handling pieces from the gold patch and includes substantial unrelated packaging churn.

Task Fitmuch worse Δ-2

It only implements part of the telemetry provenance work and does not address the Codex CLI failure-handling regression that the task explicitly calls out. The gold patch also updates config-backed attempt rows and failure paths across adapters/scheduler; the candidate does not.

Correctness Safetymuch worse Δ-2

The candidate hard-codes `usage_source`/`cost_source` for OpenAI adapters even when those fields may be absent, unlike the gold patch which derives provenance conditionally from the payload. It also leaves Codex CLI non-timeout failure handling unchanged, so command failures still do not follow the corrected behavior from gold. Missing `AttemptRow` schema fields in `config.py` creates a risk that serialized rows are inconsistent with the contract.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The gold patch centralizes provenance parsing in a helper and threads the new fields through the typed row model cleanly. The candidate duplicates string literals in individual adapters and bypasses the row contract by stuffing fields directly into serialized payloads, which is less cohesive and easier to drift. Unrelated egg-info artifacts also add noise.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

The gold patch adds focused unit coverage for OpenAI responses, OpenAI-compatible, Codex CLI provenance, and scheduler persistence. The candidate adds no tests, so the regression is not defended.

Change Focusmuch worse Δ-2

It adds multiple generated `repogauge.egg-info` files unrelated to the task. That churn is absent from the gold patch and reduces review clarity.

diff --git a/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
new file mode 100644

+++ b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
@@ -0,0 +1,134 @@
+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+Requires-Dist: PyYAML>=6.0.2
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+- [docs/junit_parser_contract.md](docs/junit_parser_contract.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--enrich-github` | disabled | Enable optional GitHub issue/PR metadata enrichment |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--github-token TOKEN` | `$(GITHUB_TOKEN)` | Token used for GitHub API calls |
+| `--github-enrichment-cache PATH` | `<out>/github_enrichment_cache.json` | Optional local cache for enrichment responses |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### Command artifact contract (current scaffold)
+
+For `--out` directory `./out`, the scaffold writes command-specific artifacts:
+
+- `manifest.json`
+  - command metadata and step status for each run invocation
+- `events.jsonl`
+  - machine-readable execution events for the same run
+- `repo_profile.json`, `scan.jsonl`, `candidates.jsonl` for `mine`
+- `reviewed.jsonl`, `review.md`, `review.html` for `review`
+- `materialized.jsonl`, `materialization_rejections.jsonl`, `dataset/dataset.jsonl`,
+  `dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl`, `adapter_<repo>.py`, `specs.json` for `export`
+- `validation.jsonl` for `eval`
+
+This list reflects what the v0.1 scaffold guarantees today; future stages
+extend it to include run-level and analysis artifacts.
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

Overall Δ

Confidence

Candidate adds part of the telemetry provenance plumbing, but misses the core propagation through adapter finalization, adds no regression tests, and includes unrelated packaging churn.

Task Fitmuch worse Δ-2

The main task was to track adapter telemetry provenance end-to-end and fix Codex CLI failure handling. While the candidate adds source fields and some parsing, it does not update the base adapter finalization paths to preserve `usage_source` and `cost_source`, so provenance can be dropped before persistence for normal adapter flows. That is a material miss relative to the gold patch.

Correctness Safetymuch worse Δ-2

Gold explicitly threads provenance through `_BaseConcreteSolverAdapter` result rewriting and keeps failed/timed-out Codex CLI attempts from surfacing partial patches. The candidate omits the base propagation changes and also returns `model_patch=text or None` plus parsed usage/cost on failed or timed-out Codex CLI runs, which increases regression risk by treating partial stdout as meaningful model output.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The helper split in gold keeps generic response parsing and Codex CLI parsing clearly separated while preserving behavior. The candidate changes `_parse_usage_cost`’s contract and partially implements the feature, which makes the code less coherent. The added `repogauge.egg-info` files also add noise that does not belong in this fix.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

Gold adds focused unit coverage for response-source tagging, Codex CLI telemetry provenance, and scheduler persistence. The candidate includes no tests, so the key regression is left unprotected.

Change Focusmuch worse Δ-2

The production changes are already incomplete, and the diff also introduces unrelated generated packaging artifacts under `repogauge.egg-info/`, which is avoidable churn outside the task scope.

diff --git a/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..657c44e
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
@@ -0,0 +1,134 @@
+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+Requires-Dist: PyYAML>=6.0.2
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+- [docs/junit_parser_contract.md](docs/junit_parser_contract.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--enrich-github` | disabled | Enable optional GitHub issue/PR metadata enrichment |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--github-token TOKEN` | `$(GITHUB_TOKEN)` | Token used for GitHub API calls |
+| `--github-enrichment-cache PATH` | `<out>/github_enrichment_cache.json` | Optional local cache for enrichment responses |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### Command artifact contract (current scaffold)
+
+For `--out` directory `./out`, the scaffold writes command-specific artifacts:
+
+- `manifest.json`
+  - command metadata and step status for each run invocation
+- `events.jsonl`
+  - machine-readable execution events for the same run
+- `repo_profile.json`, `scan.jsonl`, `candidates.jsonl` for `mine`
+- `reviewed.jsonl`, `review.md`, `review.html` for `review`
+- `materialized.jsonl`, `materialization_rejections.jsonl`, `dataset/dataset.jsonl`,
+  `dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl`, `adapter_<repo>.py`, `specs.json` for `export`
+- `validation.jsonl` for `eval`
+
+This list reflects what the v0.1 scaffold guarantees today; future stages
+extend it to include run-level and analysis artifacts.
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

Overall Δ
-1.00
Confidence
0.95

Candidate carries the schema/plumbing changes but misses key parts of the gold fix, especially Codex CLI failure handling, Anthropic provenance support, and the regression tests, while also adding unrelated packaging churn.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It only partially implements telemetry provenance and does not match the gold fix's behavior changes for Codex CLI failure handling. It also omits the Anthropic adapter provenance update and adds no corresponding regression coverage for the stated task.

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

OpenAI adapters now stamp `response.usage`/`response.cost` unconditionally instead of deriving provenance from the actual payload, which can misreport source metadata. More importantly, the Codex CLI control-flow fix from the gold patch is missing, so the candidate does not address the failure-handling regression the task calls out.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The gold patch centralizes provenance extraction with a helper and applies it consistently; the candidate duplicates hardcoded source strings in individual adapters and leaves coverage gaps. The extra checked-in `repogauge.egg-info` artifacts also increase noise and long-term maintenance burden.

Test Qualityworse Δ-1

The gold patch adds focused unit tests for OpenAI responses, OpenAI-compatible, Codex CLI provenance, and scheduler persistence. The candidate adds no tests, so it does not lock in the regression fix or the new provenance behavior.

Change Focusworse Δ-1

The production edits are only loosely scoped to the task, and the addition of multiple `repogauge.egg-info` generated files is unrelated churn absent from the gold patch.

+_PARSER_REGISTRY: Dict[str, Any] = {

+
+
+def parse_repogauge_test_output(
+    report: object, parser_name: str, test_spec: Any | None = None
+) -> Dict[str, str]:
+    """Dispatch test output parsing by parser name.
+
+    Args:
+        report: The test output payload (path, string, or mapping).
+        parser_name: Name of the registered parser to use.
+        test_spec: Optional harness-provided spec object.
+
+    Returns:
+        A canonicalized mapping of test IDs to outcomes.
+
+    Raises:
+        KeyError: if parser_name is not registered.
+    """
+    if parser_name not in _PARSER_REGISTRY:
+        raise KeyError(f"unknown test parser: {parser_name!r}")
+    return _PARSER_REGISTRY[parser_name](report, test_spec)
LLM Judgeworse
Overall Δ
-0.95
Confidence
0.87

Candidate implements the core parser-name dispatch and lazy swebench import, but it is narrower and less robust than the gold patch and appears to omit the regression tests entirely.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It adds `parse_repogauge_test_output` and exposes it, which covers the main dispatcher behavior, but it does not match the fuller gold surface area (`get_parser`, `register_parser`, default `junit` dispatch path). The narrower API means it addresses the task, but not as completely as the reference.

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

The lazy import change is correct and reduces eager dependency loading, but the dispatcher is less defensive than gold: parser names are not normalized, there is no registration pathway, and the public API requires an explicit parser name rather than safely defaulting to `junit`. Those choices increase edge-case and integration risk relative to gold.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The implementation is concise, but it relies on a module-level `Dict[str, Any]` registry and direct membership checks instead of typed parser functions and dedicated helpers for normalization and lookup. Gold is clearer about extension points and error handling.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

Compared with the gold patch, the candidate shows no added regression coverage for parser-name dispatch, unknown parser handling, or verification that the swebench parser is not eagerly imported. That is a substantial drop in testing posture.

Change Focusbetter Δ+1

The candidate keeps the production change tightly scoped to the immediate behavior and avoids the broader parser registration API added by gold. Relative to gold, there is less implementation churn outside the core fix.

+def parse_repogauge_test_output(
+    report: object,
+    *,

+    test_spec: Any | None = None,
+) -> Dict[str, str]:
+    """Dispatch test output parsing by parser name."""
+    parsers = {"junit": parse_repogauge_junit}
+    if not isinstance(parser_name, str):
+        raise KeyError(f"unknown test parser: {parser_name}")
+
+    parser = parsers.get(parser_name.strip().lower())
+    if parser is None:
+        raise KeyError(f"unknown test parser: {parser_name}")
+    return parser(report, test_spec)

diff --git a/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..5a86ef7
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
@@ -0,0 +1,112 @@
+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

+"""Harness-facing JUnit parser bridge (bead 3wi).
+
+Wraps repogauge.validation.junit_parser to accept the variety of report
+payload formats the harness may supply: Path, str, bytes, or a dict with
+a ``junit_xml`` key pointing to a Path.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Dict, Union
+
+from repogauge.validation.junit_parser import (
+    JUnitParseError,
+    _canonical_id,
+    _outcome_of,
+)
+
+
+def _parse_text(text: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
+    try:
+        root = ET.fromstring(text)
+    except ET.ParseError as exc:
+        raise JUnitParseError(f"malformed JUnit XML: {exc}") from exc
+
+    suites = root.findall(".//testsuite") or ([root] if root.tag == "testsuite" else [])
+    if not suites:
+        raise JUnitParseError("no <testsuite> elements found")
+
+    results: Dict[str, str] = {}
+    for suite in suites:
+        for tc in suite.findall("testcase"):
+            classname = (tc.get("classname") or "").strip()
+            name = (tc.get("name") or "").strip()
+            if not name:
+                continue
+            results[_canonical_id(classname, name)] = _outcome_of(tc)
+
+    return results
+
+
+def parse_repogauge_junit(payload: Union[Path, str, bytes, dict]) -> Dict[str, str]:
+    """Parse JUnit XML and return ``{test_id: outcome}``.
+
+    Accepts:
+    - ``Path``: read the file at that path
+    - ``str``: treat as raw XML text
+    - ``bytes``: decode as UTF-8, then parse
+    - ``dict``: read from ``payload["junit_xml"]`` (a Path or str path)
+
+    Raises:
+        TypeError: for any other payload type
+        JUnitParseError: if the XML is absent, empty, or malformed
+    """
+    if isinstance(payload, Path):
+        if not payload.exists():
+            raise JUnitParseError(f"JUnit XML not found: {payload}")
+        text = payload.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip()
+        if not text:
+            raise JUnitParseError(f"JUnit XML is empty: {payload}")
+    elif isinstance(payload, bytes):
+        text = payload.decode("utf-8")
+    elif isinstance(payload, str):
+        text = payload
+    elif isinstance(payload, dict):
+        xml_path = Path(payload["junit_xml"])
+        if not xml_path.exists():
+            raise JUnitParseError(f"JUnit XML not found: {xml_path}")
+        text = xml_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8").strip()
+        if not text:
+            raise JUnitParseError(f"JUnit XML is empty: {xml_path}")
+    else:
+        raise TypeError(f"unsupported report payload: {type(payload)!r}")
+
+    return _parse_text(text)

+"""Harness-facing JUnit parser bridge.
+
+This module accepts the payload shapes used by the official harness and
+normalizes them into the validation parser's file-based interface.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any, Dict
+
+from repogauge.validation.junit_parser import (
+    parse_junit_xml,
+    _parse_junit_xml_text,
+)
+
+
+def _payload_to_path_or_text(payload: Any) -> Path | str | None:
+    if isinstance(payload, bytes):
+        return payload.decode("utf-8")
+    if isinstance(payload, Path):
+        return payload
+    if isinstance(payload, str):
+        stripped = payload.lstrip()
+        candidate = Path(payload)
+        if candidate.exists() or (stripped and not stripped.startswith("<")):
+            return candidate
+        return payload
+    if isinstance(payload, dict):
+        for key in ("junit_xml", "xml", "path", "report", "payload"):
+            if key in payload:
+                return _payload_to_path_or_text(payload[key])
+    return None
+
+
+def parse_repogauge_junit(report: Any) -> Dict[str, str]:
+    """Parse a harness JUnit payload into canonical test outcomes.
+
+    Accepted payloads include:
+    - ``pathlib.Path`` instances pointing to a JUnit XML file
+    - filesystem path strings
+    - raw XML strings / bytes
+    - dict payloads containing ``junit_xml`` or common path/content keys
+    """
+    normalized = _payload_to_path_or_text(report)
+    if normalized is None:
+        raise TypeError("unsupported report payload")
+
+    if isinstance(normalized, Path):
+        return parse_junit_xml(normalized)
+    if isinstance(normalized, str) and normalized.lstrip().startswith("<"):
+        return _parse_junit_xml_text(normalized, source="<harness report>")
+    if isinstance(normalized, str):
+        return parse_junit_xml(Path(normalized))
+    return _parse_junit_xml_text(normalized, source="<bytes>")

+"""JUnit XML parser bridge for harness integration (bead 3wi).
+
+Exposes ``parse_repogauge_junit``, a polymorphic entry-point that accepts
+paths, raw XML strings/bytes, or dict payloads and returns a mapping of
+canonical test IDs to outcomes.
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any, Dict
+
+from repogauge.validation.junit_parser import (
+    JUnitParseError,
+    _canonical_id,
+    _outcome_of,
+    parse_junit_xml,
+)
+
+
+def parse_repogauge_junit(payload: Any) -> Dict[str, str]:
+    """Parse a JUnit XML payload and return ``{test_id: outcome}``.
+
+    Supported *payload* types:
+
+    - ``pathlib.Path`` -> read the file at that path.
+    - ``str`` -> parse the raw XML text.
+    - ``bytes`` -> parse the raw XML bytes.
+    - ``dict`` -> must contain the key ``"junit_xml"`` whose value is a
+      ``pathlib.Path``.
+
+    Outcomes are one of: ``"pass"``, ``"fail"``, ``"error"``, ``"skip"``.
+
+    Raises:
+        JUnitParseError: if the XML is absent, empty, or malformed.
+        TypeError: if *payload* is not one of the supported types.
+    """
+    if isinstance(payload, Path):
+        return parse_junit_xml(payload)
+
+    if isinstance(payload, dict):
+        xml_path = payload.get("junit_xml")
+        if isinstance(xml_path, Path):
+            return parse_junit_xml(xml_path)
+        raise TypeError(
+            f"unsupported report payload: {type(payload).__name__}"
+        )
+
+    if isinstance(payload, (str, bytes)):
+        try:
+            root = ET.fromstring(payload)
+        except ET.ParseError as exc:
+            raise JUnitParseError(f"malformed JUnit XML: {exc}") from exc
+
+        suites = root.findall(".//testsuite") or (
+            [root] if root.tag == "testsuite" else []
+        )
+        if not suites:
+            raise JUnitParseError("no <testsuite> elements found")
+
+        results: Dict[str, str] = {}
+        for suite in suites:
+            for tc in suite.findall("testcase"):
+                classname = (tc.get("classname") or "").strip()
+                name = (tc.get("name") or "").strip()
+                if not name:
+                    continue
+                test_id = _canonical_id(classname, name)
+                results[test_id] = _outcome_of(tc)
+        return results
+
+    raise TypeError(f"unsupported report payload: {type(payload).__name__}")

Overall Δ
-0.90
Confidence
0.95

Candidate lands the adapter hook but falls short of the gold bridge by duplicating parser logic, narrowing accepted payload shapes, and omitting the validation-layer refactor and compatibility tests that make the bridge consistent and robust.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It does wire generated adapters to `parse_repogauge_junit`, so the main integration path is covered. But it does not fully match the task intent of a generic harness bridge because it only accepts dict payloads with a `junit_xml` Path and does not support string file paths or the broader payload conventions handled by the gold patch.

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

The gold patch centralizes XML-content parsing in `repogauge.validation.junit_parser` so harness parsing stays aligned with validation semantics. The candidate instead reimplements XML parsing in `repogauge/parsers/junit.py` using private helpers, creating semantic drift risk and bypassing the validation parser’s canonical error behavior. It also rejects mapping payloads that contain XML text or alternate common keys, and a string path to an existing XML file would be misparsed as XML content rather than read from disk.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The candidate duplicates parsing logic instead of reusing a shared `parse_junit_xml_content` helper, which increases long-term maintenance cost and makes future parser changes easy to miss. It also imports private validation helpers (`_canonical_id`, `_outcome_of`) across module boundaries, which is a weaker design than the gold patch’s public helper reuse. `repogauge/parsers/__init__.py` is also incomplete relative to the gold export surface.

Test Qualityworse Δ-1

No candidate tests are shown for the new bridge behavior. The gold patch adds direct coverage for adapter generation, path/XML/bytes/dict payload handling, malformed XML propagation, and parser identity in generated adapters.

Change Focussame Δ+0

The candidate stays scoped to the parser bridge work and does not introduce obvious unrelated churn. The main issue is incompleteness and duplication, not scope creep.

+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.

diff --git a/repogauge/export/split_patch.py b/repogauge/export/split_patch.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..1c26e56
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge/export/split_patch.py
@@ -0,0 +1,99 @@
+"""Utilities for splitting a unified diff into production and test patches."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import re
+from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
+
+from repogauge.mining.file_roles import classify_file
+
+
+DIFF_HEADER_RE = re.compile(r"^diff --git (?:a/)?(.+?) (?:b/)?(.+)$")
+
+
+class PatchSplitError(RuntimeError):
+    """Raised when a patch cannot be cleanly split into prod and test components."""
+
+
+def split_prod_and_test(diff: str) -> Tuple[str, str, Dict[str, List[str]]]:
+    """Split a unified diff into production and test patches.
+
+    test_support files (conftest, fixtures, etc.) follow test files into the test
+    patch when the diff contains at least one actual test file; otherwise they fall
+    through to the prod patch.
+
+    Returns:
+        (prod_patch, test_patch, meta) where meta holds 'prod_files' and 'test_files'.
+
+    Raises:
+        PatchSplitError: if a chunk crosses the prod/test boundary (e.g. a rename).
+    """
+    chunks: list[tuple[str, list[str]]] = []
+    current_lines: list[str] | None = None
+    current_role: str = "prod"
+
+    for line in diff.splitlines(keepends=True):
+        match = DIFF_HEADER_RE.match(line)
+        if match:
+            if current_lines is not None:
+                chunks.append((current_role, current_lines))
+
+            from_path = match.group(1).strip()
+            to_path = match.group(2).strip()
+
+            from_role = classify_file(from_path).role
+            to_role = classify_file(to_path).role
+
+            from_is_test_side = from_role in {"test", "test_support"}
+            to_is_test_side = to_role in {"test", "test_support"}
+            if from_is_test_side != to_is_test_side:
+                raise PatchSplitError(
+                    f"cross-boundary rename: {from_path!r} ({from_role}) -> {to_path!r} ({to_role})"
+                )
+
+            current_role = to_role
+            current_lines = [line]
+        else:
+            if current_lines is not None:
+                current_lines.append(line)
+
+    if current_lines is not None:
+        chunks.append((current_role, current_lines))
+
+    has_test_files = any(role == "test" for role, _ in chunks)
+
+    prod_chunks: list[str] = []
+    test_chunks: list[str] = []
+    prod_files: list[str] = []
+    test_files: list[str] = []
+
+    for role, lines in chunks:
+        chunk_text = "".join(lines)
+        file_path = ""
+        m = DIFF_HEADER_RE.match(lines[0])
+        if m:
+            file_path = m.group(2).strip()
+
+        if role == "test":
+            test_chunks.append(chunk_text)
+            if file_path:
+                test_files.append(file_path)
+        elif role == "test_support":
+            if has_test_files:
+                test_chunks.append(chunk_text)
+                if file_path:
+                    test_files.append(file_path)
+            else:
+                prod_chunks.append(chunk_text)
+                if file_path:
+                    prod_files.append(file_path)
+        else:
+            prod_chunks.append(chunk_text)
+            if file_path:
+                prod_files.append(file_path)
+
+    return (
+        "".join(prod_chunks),
+        "".join(test_chunks),
+        {"prod_files": prod_files, "test_files": test_files},
+    )

Candidate adds a basic split helper, but it misses the required integration and tests and includes unrelated packaging churn, so it falls well short of the gold fix.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

The task required both shared split logic and wiring it into materialization so production/test patches are emitted and ambiguous splits are rejected with reason codes. The candidate only adds a standalone `split_patch.py` and does not update `repogauge/export/materialize.py` or add the regression tests, so it does not address the full task as the gold patch does.

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

The candidate's splitter is materially less safe than gold. It classifies boundaries only from the `diff --git` header paths instead of parsing rename metadata, so rename handling is less exact. It also omits the gold patch's explicit metadata (`test_support_files`, `all_touched_files`) and does not integrate `PatchSplitError` into materialization rejection flow, so failed/ambiguous splits would not produce the required downstream behavior.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The new helper is readable, but it is a simplified duplicate of logic that the gold patch implements more robustly. The gold version has clearer decomposition for header parsing, rename extraction, bucket assignment, and touched-file tracking, making future extension safer. Missing integration also leaves the overall change incomplete from a maintenance perspective.

Test Qualityworse Δ-1

The candidate adds no tests at all, while the gold patch adds focused unit coverage for prod/test splitting, test-support routing, and cross-boundary rename rejection. Relative to the gold fix, test posture is substantially weaker.

Change Focusworse Δ-1

The candidate introduces unrelated generated packaging artifacts (`repogauge.egg-info/*`, `uv.lock`) that are not part of the task. The gold patch is tightly scoped to the production files and regression test needed for the feature.

+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.

diff --git a/repogauge/export/split_patch.py b/repogauge/export/split_patch.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..f7eab98
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge/export/split_patch.py
@@ -0,0 +1,164 @@
+"""Split unified diffs into production and test patches."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import re
+from dataclasses import dataclass
+from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
+
+from repogauge.mining.file_roles import classify_file
+
+
+DIFF_HEADER_RE = re.compile(r"^diff --git (?:a/)?(.+?) (?:b/)?(.+)$")
+RENAME_FROM_RE = re.compile(r"^rename from (.+)$")
+RENAME_TO_RE = re.compile(r"^rename to (.+)$")
+COPY_FROM_RE = re.compile(r"^copy from (.+)$")
+COPY_TO_RE = re.compile(r"^copy to (.+)$")
+
+
+@dataclass
+class PatchSplitError(RuntimeError):
+    """Raised when a unified diff cannot be split safely."""
+
+    reason: str
+    message: str
+
+    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
+        super().__init__(self.message)
+
+
+def _path_role(path: str) -> str:
+    return classify_file(path).role
+
+
+def _is_test_role(role: str) -> bool:
+    return role == "test"
+
+
+def _is_test_support_role(role: str) -> bool:
+    return role == "test_support"
+
+
+def _chunk_bucket(role: str, *, has_test_changes: bool) -> str:
+    if _is_test_role(role):
+        return "test"
+    if _is_test_support_role(role):
+        return "test" if has_test_changes else "prod"
+    return "prod"
+
+
+def _raise_rename_boundary_error(old_path: str, new_path: str) -> None:
+    old_role = _path_role(old_path)
+    new_role = _path_role(new_path)
+    if (_is_test_role(old_role) or _is_test_support_role(old_role)) != (
+        _is_test_role(new_role) or _is_test_support_role(new_role)
+    ):
+        raise PatchSplitError(
+            reason="cross_boundary_rename",
+            message=f"rename across production/test boundary is not supported: {old_path} -> {new_path}",
+        )
+
+
+def _inspect_for_rename_markers(chunk_lines: List[str]) -> None:
+    rename_from: Optional[str] = None
+    rename_to: Optional[str] = None
+    copy_from: Optional[str] = None
+    copy_to: Optional[str] = None
+
+    for line in chunk_lines:
+        if rename_from is None:
+            match = RENAME_FROM_RE.match(line)
+            if match:
+                rename_from = match.group(1).strip()
+                continue
+        if rename_to is None:
+            match = RENAME_TO_RE.match(line)
+            if match:
+                rename_to = match.group(1).strip()
+                continue
+        if copy_from is None:
+            match = COPY_FROM_RE.match(line)
+            if match:
+                copy_from = match.group(1).strip()
+                continue
+        if copy_to is None:
+            match = COPY_TO_RE.match(line)
+            if match:
+                copy_to = match.group(1).strip()
+
+    if rename_from and rename_to:
+        _raise_rename_boundary_error(rename_from, rename_to)
+    if copy_from and copy_to:
+        _raise_rename_boundary_error(copy_from, copy_to)
+
+
+def split_prod_and_test(diff: str) -> Tuple[str, str, Dict[str, Any]]:
+    """Split a unified diff into production and test patches.
+
+    The function preserves the exact diff text for each chunk. Test-support
+    files are routed with test changes when the patch includes at least one
+    explicit test file; otherwise they remain with production changes.
+    """
+
+    chunks: list[tuple[str, List[str], List[str]]] = []
+    current_header: Optional[str] = None
+    current_lines: List[str] = []
+    current_paths: List[str] = []
+
+    def flush() -> None:
+        nonlocal current_header, current_lines, current_paths
+        if current_header is None:
+            return
+        chunks.append((current_header, current_paths[:], current_lines[:]))
+        current_header = None
+        current_lines = []
+        current_paths = []
+
+    for line in diff.splitlines(keepends=True):
+        header_match = DIFF_HEADER_RE.match(line)
+        if header_match:
+            flush()
+            current_header = line
+            current_lines = [line]
+            current_paths = [header_match.group(1).strip(), header_match.group(2).strip()]
+            continue
+
+        if current_header is None:
+            # Preserve any leading diff prologue with the production patch.
+            current_header = ""
+            current_lines = [line]
+            current_paths = []
+        else:
+            current_lines.append(line)
+
+    flush()
+
+    has_test_changes = any(_is_test_role(classify_file(path).role) for _, paths, _ in chunks for path in paths if path)
+
+    prod_chunks: list[str] = []
+    test_chunks: list[str] = []
+    touched: Dict[str, List[str]] = {"prod": [], "test": [], "unknown": []}
+
+    for header, paths, lines in chunks:
+        if header:
+            _inspect_for_rename_markers(lines)
+
+        # Prefer the b/ path when present, but keep both sides for rename checks.
+        file_path = paths[1] if len(paths) > 1 and paths[1] else (paths[0] if paths else "")
+        role = classify_file(file_path).role if file_path else "unknown"
+        bucket = _chunk_bucket(role, has_test_changes=has_test_changes)
+
+        bucket_name = bucket if bucket in {"prod", "test"} else "unknown"
+        if file_path and file_path not in touched[bucket_name]:
+            touched[bucket_name].append(file_path)
+
+        rendered = "".join(lines)
+        if bucket == "test":
+            test_chunks.append(rendered)
+        else:
+            prod_chunks.append(rendered)
+
+    return "".join(prod_chunks), "".join(test_chunks), {
+        "prod_files": touched["prod"],
+        "test_files": touched["test"],
+    }

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.

diff --git a/repogauge/export/split_patch.py b/repogauge/export/split_patch.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..1ef9c66
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge/export/split_patch.py
@@ -0,0 +1,113 @@
+"""Unified diff splitting into production and test patches."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import re
+from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
+
+from repogauge.mining.file_roles import classify_file
+
+DIFF_HEADER_RE = re.compile(r"^diff --git (?:a/)?(.+?) (?:b/)?(.+)$")
+
+
+class PatchSplitError(RuntimeError):
+    """Raised when a patch cannot be split into production and test patches."""
+
+
+def _parse_chunks(diff: str) -> List[List[str]]:
+    """Split a unified diff into chunks per file."""
+    chunks: List[List[str]] = []
+    current_chunk: List[str] = []
+    for line in diff.splitlines(keepends=True):
+        if DIFF_HEADER_RE.match(line):
+            if current_chunk:
+                chunks.append(current_chunk)
+            current_chunk = [line]
+        else:
+            current_chunk.append(line)
+    if current_chunk:
+        chunks.append(current_chunk)
+    return chunks
+
+
+def _is_rename(chunk: List[str]) -> bool:
+    """Detect if a diff chunk represents a rename."""
+    return any("rename from " in line or "rename to " in line for line in chunk)
+
+
+def _is_test_realm(role: str) -> bool:
+    return role in ("test", "test_support")
+
+
+def split_prod_and_test(diff: str) -> Tuple[str, str, Dict[str, List[str]]]:
+    """Split a unified diff into production and test patches.
+
+    Test-support files are placed in the test patch only when there are
+    actual test file changes in the diff. Otherwise they remain in the
+    production patch.
+
+    Cross-category renames (between production and test realms) are
+    rejected with :class:`PatchSplitError`.
+
+    Returns:
+        Tuple of (prod_patch, test_patch, metadata) where metadata
+        contains ``prod_files`` and ``test_files`` lists.
+    """
+    chunks = _parse_chunks(diff)
+
+    chunk_infos: List[Tuple[List[str], str, str]] = []
+
+    for chunk in chunks:
+        header = chunk[0]
+        match = DIFF_HEADER_RE.match(header)
+        if not match:
+            raise PatchSplitError("Missing diff header in chunk")
+
+        a_path = match.group(1).strip()
+        b_path = match.group(2).strip()
+
+        a_role = classify_file(a_path).role
+        b_role = classify_file(b_path).role
+
+        if _is_rename(chunk):
+            a_is_test = _is_test_realm(a_role)
+            b_is_test = _is_test_realm(b_role)
+            if a_is_test != b_is_test:
+                raise PatchSplitError(
+                    f"Cross-category rename from {a_path} to {b_path}"
+                )
+
+        chunk_infos.append((chunk, b_path, b_role))
+
+    has_test_changes = any(role == "test" for _, _, role in chunk_infos)
+
+    prod_chunks: List[List[str]] = []
+    test_chunks: List[List[str]] = []
+    touched: Dict[str, List[str]] = {"prod": [], "test": []}
+
+    for chunk, path, role in chunk_infos:
+        if role == "test":
+            test_chunks.append(chunk)
+            if path not in touched["test"]:
+                touched["test"].append(path)
+        elif role == "test_support":
+            if has_test_changes:
+                test_chunks.append(chunk)
+                if path not in touched["test"]:
+                    touched["test"].append(path)
+            else:
+                prod_chunks.append(chunk)
+                if path not in touched["prod"]:
+                    touched["prod"].append(path)
+        else:
+            prod_chunks.append(chunk)
+            if path not in touched["prod"]:
+                touched["prod"].append(path)
+
+    prod_patch = "".join("".join(chunk) for chunk in prod_chunks)
+    test_patch = "".join("".join(chunk) for chunk in test_chunks)
+
+    return prod_patch, test_patch, {
+        "prod_files": touched["prod"],
+        "test_files": touched["test"],
+    }

+version = 1

LLM Judgemuch worse
Overall Δ
-1.25
Confidence
0.88

Candidate captures the basic extraction refactor but falls short of the gold fix on split robustness, rejection semantics, and test coverage, with substantial unrelated churn.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It moves split logic into a shared module and wires materialization through it, but it does not match the gold behavior fully: rejection uses a generic `patch_split_failed` reason instead of the expected specific unsupported-rename reason code, and it omits the richer split metadata the gold patch records.

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

The candidate splitter handles simple file-chunk separation, but it is less safe than gold for exact diff preservation and edge cases. The gold parser uses shell-style header parsing and explicit rename path extraction, which is safer for quoted paths and rename headers; the candidate relies on a regex and broad rename detection. It also misses the gold special handling for helper files like `conftest.py`/`pytest.ini`/`tox.ini` and does not preserve `test_support_files`/`all_touched_files` metadata.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The refactor is directionally good, but the implementation is thinner and less explicit than gold about boundary cases and output metadata. The gold patch has clearer decomposition around header parsing, rename extraction, bucket assignment, and error typing, making future extension safer.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

The gold patch adds focused regression tests covering prod/test chunk splitting, test-support inclusion rules, keeping support files in prod when no tests change, and cross-boundary rename rejection. The candidate patch adds no corresponding tests at all.

Change Focusmuch worse Δ-2

The candidate includes substantial unrelated churn: review artifacts, `repogauge.egg-info/*`, and `uv.lock`. The gold patch is tightly scoped to the production files and one targeted test file.

+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+- [docs/junit_parser_contract.md](docs/junit_parser_contract.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--enrich-github` | disabled | Enable optional GitHub issue/PR metadata enrichment |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--github-token TOKEN` | `$(GITHUB_TOKEN)` | Token used for GitHub API calls |
+| `--github-enrichment-cache PATH` | `<out>/github_enrichment_cache.json` | Optional local cache for enrichment responses |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### Command artifact contract (current scaffold)
+
+For `--out` directory `./out`, the scaffold writes command-specific artifacts:
+
+- `manifest.json`
+  - command metadata and step status for each run invocation
+- `events.jsonl`
+  - machine-readable execution events for the same run
+- `repo_profile.json`, `scan.jsonl`, `candidates.jsonl` for `mine`
+- `reviewed.jsonl`, `review.md`, `review.html` for `review`
+- `materialized.jsonl`, `materialization_rejections.jsonl`, `dataset/dataset.jsonl`,
+  `dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl`, `adapter_<repo>.py`, `specs.json` for `export`
+- `validation.jsonl` for `eval`
+
+This list reflects what the v0.1 scaffold guarantees today; future stages
+extend it to include run-level and analysis artifacts.
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

The gold patch adds targeted tests for required fields, importability, registration maps, and deterministic generation. No corresponding candidate test updates are shown, so the new behavior is materially less protected against regression.

The candidate introduces multiple generated packaging files unrelated to the bead's adapter-registration task. That extra churn is absent from the gold patch and makes the diff substantially less disciplined.

+++ b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
@@ -0,0 +1,133 @@
+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+- [docs/junit_parser_contract.md](docs/junit_parser_contract.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--enrich-github` | disabled | Enable optional GitHub issue/PR metadata enrichment |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--github-token TOKEN` | `$(GITHUB_TOKEN)` | Token used for GitHub API calls |
+| `--github-enrichment-cache PATH` | `<out>/github_enrichment_cache.json` | Optional local cache for enrichment responses |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### Command artifact contract (current scaffold)
+
+For `--out` directory `./out`, the scaffold writes command-specific artifacts:
+
+- `manifest.json`
+  - command metadata and step status for each run invocation
+- `events.jsonl`
+  - machine-readable execution events for the same run
+- `repo_profile.json`, `scan.jsonl`, `candidates.jsonl` for `mine`
+- `reviewed.jsonl`, `review.md`, `review.html` for `review`
+- `materialized.jsonl`, `materialization_rejections.jsonl`, `dataset/dataset.jsonl`,
+  `dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl`, `adapter_<repo>.py`, `specs.json` for `export`
+- `validation.jsonl` for `eval`
+
+This list reflects what the v0.1 scaffold guarantees today; future stages
+extend it to include run-level and analysis artifacts.
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

LLM Judgemuch worse
Overall Δ
-1.25
Confidence
0.86

Candidate implements adapter registration data, but diverges from the gold contract, omits the targeted tests, and adds unrelated packaging artifacts.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It covers the core idea of adding version/module metadata and registration maps, but it does not match the gold patch's registration payload shape. In particular, `registration_context()` omits the map bundle expected by the gold solution, and the generated map spec uses a different structure (`test_cmd` instead of the gold's `test_cmd_base` plus `strategy_name`).

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

The candidate leaves `_safe_module_name()` unchanged, so edge cases the gold fix handles (empty repo name, leading digit, stricter sanitization) remain exposed. It also changes the serialized/runtime contract by embedding a richer `docker_specs` object and different version-spec contents, which increases compatibility risk versus the gold implementation.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The gold patch keeps the generated registration data declarative and directly rendered from the spec. The candidate instead initializes empty dicts and mutates them at import time, while also duplicating overlapping fields across `docker_specs` and top-level spec content. That is less clear and makes the generated adapter contract harder to reason about.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

The gold patch adds focused unit coverage for the new fields, importability, registration maps, and determinism. No corresponding test updates are present in the candidate diff, so the new behavior is materially less protected.

Change Focusmuch worse Δ-2

The task is confined to `repogauge/export/adapter.py` and `tests/unit/test_adapter.py`, but the candidate also adds multiple `repogauge.egg-info` files unrelated to the regression. That is clear scope creep compared with the gold patch's disciplined change set.

+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### Command artifact contract (current scaffold)
+
+For `--out` directory `./out`, the scaffold writes command-specific artifacts:
+
+- `manifest.json`
+  - command metadata and step status for each run invocation
+- `events.jsonl`
+  - machine-readable execution events for the same run
+- `repo_profile.json`, `scan.jsonl`, `candidates.jsonl` for `mine`
+- `reviewed.jsonl`, `review.md`, `review.html` for `review`
+- `materialized.jsonl`, `materialization_rejections.jsonl`, `dataset/dataset.jsonl`,
+  `dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl`, `adapter_<repo>.py`, `specs.json` for `export`
+- `validation.jsonl` for `eval`
+
+This list reflects what the v0.1 scaffold guarantees today; future stages
+extend it to include run-level and analysis artifacts.
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.

diff --git a/repogauge/validation/env_detect.py b/repogauge/validation/env_detect.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..d8a9a51
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge/validation/env_detect.py
@@ -0,0 +1,114 @@
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass
+from typing import Any
+
+
+@dataclass
+class EnvPlan:
+    python_version: str
+    pre_install: list[str]
+    install: list[str]
+    build: list[str]
+    test_cmd_base: str
+    strategy_name: str
+    confidence: float
+    provenance: list[str]
+
+    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return {
+            "python_version": self.python_version,
+            "pre_install": self.pre_install,
+            "install": self.install,
+            "build": self.build,
+            "test_cmd_base": self.test_cmd_base,
+            "strategy_name": self.strategy_name,
+            "confidence": self.confidence,
+            "provenance": self.provenance,
+        }
+
+
+def _sort_versions(versions: list[str]) -> list[str]:
+    return sorted(versions, key=lambda v: tuple(int(x) for x in v.split(".")))
+
+
+def build_environment_plan(profile: dict[str, Any]) -> EnvPlan:
+    python_hints = profile.get("python_hints", {})
+    versions = python_hints.get("versions", [])
+    package_managers = python_hints.get("package_managers", [])
+    install_hints = profile.get("install_hints", [])
+    test_commands = profile.get("test_runner_hints", {}).get("commands", [])
+
+    provenance: list[str] = []
+    confidence = 1.0
+
+    if len(versions) > 1:
+        provenance.append("python_version:conflict")
+        provenance.append("python_version:chose-minimum")
+        python_version = _sort_versions(versions)[0]
+        confidence -= 0.1
+    elif versions:
+        python_version = versions[0]
+    else:
+        python_version = "3.11"
+
+    install: list[str] = []
+    install_strategy: str
+
+    if "poetry" in package_managers:
+        install_strategy = "poetry"
+        install.append("poetry install")
+        for hint in install_hints:
+            if hint != "poetry install" and hint.startswith("pip install -e"):
+                install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:poetry")
+    elif "setuptools" in package_managers:
+        install_strategy = "setuptools"
+        install = ["pip install -e ."]
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:setuptools")
+    elif "requirements" in package_managers:
+        install_strategy = "requirements"
+        req_hints = sorted(h for h in install_hints if h.startswith("pip install -r"))
+        if req_hints:
+            install.append(req_hints[0])
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:requirements")
+    else:
+        install_strategy = "fallback"
+        install = list(install_hints) if install_hints else ["pip install -e ."]
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:fallback")
+
+    test_strategy: str
+    if "pytest" in test_commands:
+        test_cmd_base = "pytest"
+        test_strategy = "pytest"
+        provenance.append("test_runner:pytest")
+    elif "python -m unittest" in test_commands:
+        test_cmd_base = "python -m unittest"
+        test_strategy = "unittest"
+        provenance.append("test_runner:unittest")
+    elif "tox" in test_commands:
+        test_cmd_base = "tox"
+        test_strategy = "tox"
+        provenance.append("test_runner:tox")
+    elif "nox" in test_commands:
+        test_cmd_base = "nox"
+        test_strategy = "nox"
+        provenance.append("test_runner:nox")
+    else:
+        test_cmd_base = "python -m pytest"
+        test_strategy = "pytest-default"
+        provenance.append("test_runner:pytest-default")
+
+    if install_strategy == "requirements" and test_strategy in ("pytest", "pytest-default"):
+        install.append("pip install pytest")
+
+    return EnvPlan(
+        python_version=python_version,
+        pre_install=[],
+        install=install,
+        build=[],
+        test_cmd_base=test_cmd_base,
+        strategy_name=f"{install_strategy}:{test_strategy}",
+        confidence=confidence,
+        provenance=provenance,
+    )

+            cleaned = key_match.group(2).strip()
+            return cleaned or None
     return None
