+"""Deterministic environment plan synthesis."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import asdict, dataclass, field
+from typing import Any, Iterable
+
+
+def _as_sorted_unique(values: Iterable[str]) -> list[str]:
+    return sorted({str(value).strip() for value in values if str(value).strip()})
+
+
+def _version_key(version: str) -> tuple[int, ...]:
+    parts: list[int] = []
+    for chunk in str(version).strip().split("."):
+        if not chunk.isdigit():
+            break
+        parts.append(int(chunk))
+    return tuple(parts) if parts else (0,)
+
+
+def _pick_python_version(versions: list[str], provenance: list[str]) -> str:
+    normalized = _as_sorted_unique(versions)
+    if not normalized:
+        provenance.append("python_version:default-3.11")
+        return "3.11"
+    if len(normalized) > 1:
+        provenance.append("python_version:conflict")
+        chosen = min(normalized, key=_version_key)
+        provenance.append("python_version:chose-minimum")
+        return chosen
+    return normalized[0]
+
+
+def _pick_install_strategy(package_managers: list[str], install_hints: list[str], provenance: list[str]) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:
+    managers = _as_sorted_unique(package_managers)
+    hints = _as_sorted_unique(install_hints)
+
+    if "poetry" in managers:
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:poetry")
+        command = next((hint for hint in hints if hint.startswith("poetry ")), "poetry install")
+        return "poetry", [command]
+    if "uv" in managers:
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:uv")
+        command = next((hint for hint in hints if hint.startswith("uv ")), "uv sync")
+        return "uv", [command]
+    if "pipenv" in managers:
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:pipenv")
+        command = next((hint for hint in hints if hint.startswith("pipenv ")), "pipenv install")
+        return "pipenv", [command]
+    if "setuptools" in managers:
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:setuptools")
+        command = next((hint for hint in hints if hint == "pip install -e ."), "pip install -e .")
+        return "setuptools", [command]
+    if "requirements" in managers:
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:requirements")
+        command = next((hint for hint in hints if hint.startswith("pip install -r ")), "pip install -e .")
+        return "requirements", [command]
+
+    provenance.append("install_strategy:fallback")
+    command = next((hint for hint in hints if hint == "pip install -e ."), "pip install -e .")
+    return "fallback", [command]
+
+
+def _pick_test_runner(test_commands: list[str], provenance: list[str]) -> tuple[str, str]:
+    commands = _as_sorted_unique(test_commands)
+
+    if "pytest" in commands:
+        provenance.append("test_runner:pytest")
+        return "pytest", "pytest"
+    if "python -m unittest" in commands:
+        provenance.append("test_runner:unittest")
+        return "unittest", "python -m unittest"
+    if "python -m pytest" in commands:
+        provenance.append("test_runner:python-m-pytest")
+        return "pytest", "python -m pytest"
+    if "tox" in commands:
+        provenance.append("test_runner:tox")
+        return "tox", "tox"
+    if "nox" in commands:
+        provenance.append("test_runner:nox")
+        return "nox", "nox"
+
+    provenance.append("test_runner:pytest-default")
+    return "pytest-default", "python -m pytest"
+
+
+@dataclass
+class EnvPlan:
+    python_version: str
+    pre_install: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+    install: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+    build: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+    test_cmd_base: str = ""
+    strategy_name: str = ""
+    confidence: float = 0.0
+    provenance: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+
+    def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
+        return asdict(self)
+
+
+def build_environment_plan(profile: dict[str, Any]) -> EnvPlan:
+    python_hints = profile.get("python_hints", {}) or {}
+    test_runner_hints = profile.get("test_runner_hints", {}) or {}
+    install_hints = list(profile.get("install_hints", []) or [])
+
+    provenance: list[str] = []
+    python_version = _pick_python_version(list(python_hints.get("versions", []) or []), provenance)
+    install_strategy, install_cmds = _pick_install_strategy(
+        list(python_hints.get("package_managers", []) or []),
+        install_hints,
+        provenance,
+    )
+    test_strategy, test_cmd_base = _pick_test_runner(
+        list(test_runner_hints.get("commands", []) or []),
+        provenance,
+    )
+
+    if test_strategy in {"pytest", "pytest-default"} and install_strategy not in {"tox", "nox"}:
+        if all("pytest" not in command for command in install_cmds):
+            install_cmds.append("pip install pytest")
+
+    confidence = 0.85
+    if len(_as_sorted_unique(python_hints.get("versions", []) or [])) <= 1:
+        confidence += 0.05
+    if install_strategy in {"poetry", "setuptools", "requirements"}:
+        confidence += 0.05
+    if test_strategy in {"pytest", "unittest", "tox", "nox"}:
+        confidence += 0.05
+    if any(item.startswith("python_version:conflict") for item in provenance):
+        confidence -= 0.1
+
+    return EnvPlan(
+        python_version=python_version,
+        pre_install=[],
+        install=install_cmds,
+        build=[],
+        test_cmd_base=test_cmd_base,
+        strategy_name=f"{install_strategy}:{test_strategy}",
+        confidence=max(0.0, min(1.0, confidence)),
+        provenance=provenance,
+    )
+
+
+__all__ = ["EnvPlan", "build_environment_plan"]

diff --git a/repogauge/validation/env_detect.py b/repogauge/validation/env_detect.py

+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+from typing import Any
+
+
+@dataclass
+class EnvPlan:
+    python_version: str
+    pre_install: list[str]
+    install: list[str]
+    build: list[str]
+    test_cmd_base: str
+    strategy_name: str
+    confidence: float
+    provenance: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
+
+
+def build_environment_plan(profile: dict[str, Any]) -> EnvPlan:
+    """Convert repo inspection hints into a concrete install and test environment plan."""
+    python_hints = profile.get("python_hints", {}) or {}
+    install_hints = list(profile.get("install_hints", []))
+    test_runner_hints = profile.get("test_runner_hints", {}) or {}
+
+    versions = list(python_hints.get("versions", []))
+    package_managers = list(python_hints.get("package_managers", []))
+    test_commands = list(test_runner_hints.get("commands", []))
+
+    provenance: list[str] = []
+    confidence = 1.0
+
+    # Python version resolution
+    if not versions:
+        python_version = "3.10"
+        provenance.append("python_version:default")
+        confidence -= 0.1
+    elif len(versions) == 1:
+        python_version = versions[0]
+        provenance.append("python_version:explicit")
+    else:
+        def _version_key(v: str) -> tuple[int, ...]:
+            return tuple(int(p) for p in v.split(".") if p.isdigit())
+        python_version = min(versions, key=_version_key)
+        provenance.append("python_version:conflict")
+        provenance.append("python_version:chose-minimum")
+        confidence -= 0.1
+
+    # Package manager priority
+    priority = ["poetry", "pipenv", "uv", "setuptools", "requirements", "pep621", "pyproject"]
+    strategy = "unknown"
+    for pm in priority:
+        if pm in package_managers:
+            strategy = pm
+            break
+    if not package_managers:
+        strategy = "fallback"
+        confidence -= 0.1
+
+    # Determine install commands based on strategy
+    install: list[str] = []
+    pip_based_original = any("pip install" in hint for hint in install_hints)
+
+    if strategy == "poetry":
+        poetry_hints = [h for h in install_hints if "poetry" in h]
+        install.extend(poetry_hints if poetry_hints else ["poetry install"])
+        if _is_pytest_runner(test_commands) and pip_based_original:
+            install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:poetry")
+    elif strategy == "setuptools":
+        setuptools_hints = [h for h in install_hints if "pip install -e ." in h]
+        install.extend(setuptools_hints if setuptools_hints else ["pip install -e ."])
+        if _is_pytest_runner(test_commands):
+            install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:setuptools")
+    elif strategy == "requirements":
+        req_hints = [h for h in install_hints if "requirements" in h]
+        install.extend(req_hints[:1] if req_hints else ["pip install -r requirements.txt"])
+        if _is_pytest_runner(test_commands) or _is_default_pytest(test_commands):
+            install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:requirements")
+    elif strategy == "pep621":
+        pep_hints = [h for h in install_hints if "pip install" in h]
+        install.extend(pep_hints[:1] if pep_hints else ["pip install -e ."])
+        if _is_pytest_runner(test_commands):
+            install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:pep621")
+    elif strategy == "pipenv":
+        pipenv_hints = [h for h in install_hints if "pipenv" in h]
+        install.extend(pipenv_hints if pipenv_hints else ["pipenv install"])
+        if _is_pytest_runner(test_commands) and pip_based_original:
+            install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:pipenv")
+    elif strategy == "uv":
+        uv_hints = [h for h in install_hints if "uv" in h]
+        install.extend(uv_hints if uv_hints else ["uv sync"])
+        if _is_pytest_runner(test_commands) and pip_based_original:
+            install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append("install_strategy:uv")
+    else:
+        if install_hints:
+            install.append(install_hints[0])
+        else:
+            install.append("pip install -e .")
+        if _is_pytest_runner(test_commands) or _is_default_pytest(test_commands):
+            install.append("pip install pytest")
+        provenance.append(f"install_strategy:{strategy}")
+
+    # Deduplicate install commands while preserving order
+    seen: set[str] = set()
+    deduped_install: list[str] = []
+    for cmd in install:
+        if cmd not in seen:
+            seen.add(cmd)
+            deduped_install.append(cmd)
+    install = deduped_install
+
+    # Test runner resolution
+    if not test_commands:
+        test_cmd_base = "python -m pytest"
+        runner_label = "pytest-default"
+        confidence -= 0.05
+        provenance.append("test_runner:default")
+    else:
+        test_cmd_base = test_commands[0]
+        runner_label = _normalize_runner_label(test_cmd_base)
+        provenance.append(f"test_runner:{runner_label}")
+
+    strategy_name = f"{strategy}:{runner_label}"
+
+    # Confidence adjustments for non-modern stacks
+    if strategy in ("setuptools", "requirements", "fallback", "unknown"):
+        confidence -= 0.05
+    if runner_label not in ("pytest", "pytest-default"):
+        confidence -= 0.05
+
+    # Multiple package managers or test runners reduce confidence
+    if len(package_managers) > 1:
+        confidence -= 0.05
+    if len(test_commands) > 1:
+        confidence -= 0.05
+
+    return EnvPlan(
+        python_version=python_version,
+        pre_install=[],
+        install=install,
+        build=[],
+        test_cmd_base=test_cmd_base,
+        strategy_name=strategy_name,
+        confidence=round(confidence, 2),
+        provenance=provenance,
+    )
+
+
+def _is_pytest_runner(commands: list[str]) -> bool:
+    return any("pytest" in cmd.lower() for cmd in commands)
+
+
+def _is_default_pytest(commands: list[str]) -> bool:
+    return not commands
+
+
+def _normalize_runner_label(command: str) -> str:
+    lower = command.lower()
+    if "pytest" in lower:
+        return "pytest"
+    if "unittest" in lower:
+        return "unittest"
+    if "tox" in lower:
+        return "tox"
+    if "nox" in lower:
+        return "nox"
+    return "unknown"

Candidate implements the core environment-plan feature but misses parts of the gold contract, weakens determinism in several heuristics, and omits the regression tests added by the reference patch.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It adds `environment_plan` generation and an `EnvPlan` model, but it does not match the full gold-facing API because `repogauge.validation.__init__` fails to export `build_environment_plan`. It also diverges from the expected deterministic defaults and selection rules, so it addresses the task only partially relative to the gold patch.

Correctness Safetymuch worse Δ-2

Several behaviors differ materially from the gold implementation: default Python falls back to `3.10` instead of `3.11`; test-runner selection depends on first command order instead of deterministic priority; pytest dependency injection is conditional on pip-like install hints for some strategies, unlike the gold logic; and the function accepts only `dict[str, Any]` rather than coercing arbitrary profile shapes safely. These differences increase regression risk and make the plan less reliably consumable by later deterministic stages.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The candidate is readable, but it reimplements serialization with `dataclasses.asdict(...)` at the call site instead of keeping a `to_dict()` method on `EnvPlan`, omits the explicit package export for `build_environment_plan`, and hard-codes more ad hoc branching than the gold helper decomposition. The gold patch is more cohesive and easier to extend safely.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

The candidate patch includes no tests, while the gold patch adds targeted unit coverage for plan construction, package export/import behavior, and repository inspection integration. That leaves important regressions around defaults, provenance, and deterministic selection unguarded.

Change Focussame Δ+0

The patch stays focused on the environment-detection feature area and does not introduce obvious unrelated churn. Its scope discipline is comparable to the gold patch even though it is less complete.

+def _pytest_command_attempts(test_cmd_base: str) -> List[List[str]]:
+    """Return an ordered list of command argv prefixes to try for running pytest.
+
+    The first entry is the command as parsed; the second is a fallback that
+    invokes pytest via the current Python interpreter (``python -m pytest``).
+    The fallback is omitted when the original command already uses a Python
+    interpreter directly.
+    """
+    parts = shlex.split(test_cmd_base) if test_cmd_base.strip() else ["pytest"]
+    attempts: List[List[str]] = [parts]
+    if parts and not re.match(r"^python3?(\.\d+)?$", parts[0]):
+        rest = parts[1:]
+        attempts.append([sys.executable, "-m", "pytest"] + rest)
+    return attempts
+

Candidate implements a basic retry path for pytest, but it is materially less complete and less safe than the gold fix because it omits attempt propagation/telemetry, uses a broader and sometimes incorrect fallback rewrite, and adds no regression tests.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

     return parts
 
 
+def _pytest_command_attempts(test_cmd_base: str) -> List[List[str]]:
+    """Return deterministic pytest command attempts.
+
+    The first attempt is the requested command, normalized to the current Python
+    interpreter when it starts with a bare ``python`` token.  The fallback is an
+    interpreter-based ``python -m pytest`` invocation that preserves the pytest
+    arguments from the original command.
+    """
+    parts = _resolve_test_cmd(test_cmd_base)
+    if not parts:
+        parts = [sys.executable, "-m", "pytest"]
+
+    attempts: List[List[str]] = [parts]
+
+    if parts[:3] == [sys.executable, "-m", "pytest"]:
+        return attempts
+
+    if parts and parts[0] == "pytest":
+        fallback = [sys.executable, "-m", "pytest", *parts[1:]]
+    elif len(parts) >= 3 and parts[1:3] == ["-m", "pytest"]:
+        fallback = [sys.executable, "-m", "pytest", *parts[3:]]
+    else:
+        fallback = [sys.executable, "-m", "pytest", *parts[1:]]
+
+    if fallback != attempts[0]:
+        attempts.append(fallback)
+
+    return attempts
+

LLM Judgeworse
Overall Δ
-1.05
Confidence
0.90

Candidate covers the main adapter templating path but is weaker than the gold patch on robustness and regression protection, mainly due to missing tests and looser handling of adapter template vars.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It generalizes parser, extension, and install join behavior, so it addresses the core task, but it does not fully normalize/store parser import metadata in the spec the way the gold patch does. That makes future language support depend partly on extra logic in `_render_adapter` rather than solely on `harness_template_vars()` outputs.

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

The candidate swallows `ImportError` and `KeyError` and silently falls back to Python defaults, which can mask configuration mistakes for non-Python adapters. It also does not validate that `harness_template_vars()` returns a mapping, and it recomputes template vars in `_render_adapter` instead of relying on a normalized spec. Those choices increase regression risk versus the gold patch's stricter, more explicit handling.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The gold patch centralizes adapter-derived values into the spec and keeps `_render_adapter` simpler. The candidate duplicates adapter lookup/template-var handling across `build_adapter_spec` and `_render_adapter`, mixes fallback behavior into both places, and leaves parser import normalization more ad hoc, which is harder to reason about long term.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

The provided candidate diff includes no test updates, while the gold patch adds a targeted regression test proving that language adapter template vars drive parser import, parser name, extension, and install string behavior for a non-Python adapter. This is a significant gap relative to the gold solution.

Change Focussame Δ+0

The candidate stays within the intended files and problem area, with no obvious unrelated churn. The main issue is completeness and rigor, not scope discipline.

@@ -0,0 +1,54 @@
+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.

diff --git a/repogauge/mining/synthesize.py b/repogauge/mining/synthesize.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..1f702d3
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge/mining/synthesize.py
@@ -0,0 +1,86 @@
+"""Problem statement synthesis for dataset instances."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
+
+
+def synthesize_problem_statement(
+    record: Dict[str, Any],
+    patch: str = "",
+) -> Tuple[str, str, Optional[str]]:
+    """Return (statement, source, source_ref) for a candidate record.
+
+    Priority order:
+      1. linked issue title/body
+      2. PR title/body
+      3. commit message plus diff summary
+      4. LLM-generated advisory (only when commit subject is too weak)
+    """
+    metadata = record.get("metadata") or {}
+
+    def _get(key: str) -> Any:
+        val = record.get(key)
+        if val is not None:
+            return val
+        return metadata.get(key)
+
+    # 1. Linked issue
+    issue_title = _get("issue_title")
+    if issue_title:
+        issue_body = _get("issue_body") or ""
+        issue_refs: List[Any] = _get("issue_refs") or []
+        parts = [str(issue_title)]
+        if issue_body:
+            parts.append(str(issue_body))
+        source_ref = str(issue_refs[0]) if issue_refs else None
+        return "\n\n".join(parts), "linked_issue", source_ref
+
+    # 2. Pull request
+    pr_title = _get("pr_title")
+    if pr_title:
+        pr_body = _get("pr_body") or ""
+        parts = [str(pr_title)]
+        if pr_body:
+            parts.append(str(pr_body))
+        return "\n\n".join(parts), "pull_request", None
+
+    # 3. Commit message — weak single-word subjects fall through to LLM advisory
+    source_subject = _get("source_subject")
+    source_body = _get("source_body")
+
+    is_weak = bool(source_subject) and len(str(source_subject).strip().split()) <= 1
+
+    if is_weak:
+        llm_advisory = metadata.get("llm_advisory") or {}
+        llm_problem = llm_advisory.get("problem_statement")
+        if llm_problem:
+            llm_model = metadata.get("llm_model")
+            return str(llm_problem), "llm_advisory", str(llm_model) if llm_model else None
+
+    # 4. Generate commit-based statement
+    file_roles: Dict[str, Any] = metadata.get("file_roles") or {}
+    prod_files: List[str] = file_roles.get("prod") or []
+    test_files: List[str] = file_roles.get("test") or []
+    total_changed_lines = metadata.get("total_changed_lines") or len(patch.splitlines())
+
+    lines = ["Observed behavior"]
+    if source_subject and not is_weak:
+        lines.append(str(source_subject))
+    if source_body:
+        lines.append(str(source_body))
+
+    if prod_files or test_files:
+        prod_str = ", ".join(prod_files)
+        test_str = ", ".join(test_files)
+        if prod_str and test_str:
+            lines.append(f"- Production changes: {prod_str}. Test changes: {test_str}.")
+        elif prod_str:
+            lines.append(f"- Production changes: {prod_str}.")
+        else:
+            lines.append(f"- Test changes: {test_str}.")
+
+    lines.append(f"- Reproduction: run tests impacted by this change ({total_changed_lines} changed lines).")
+    lines.append("- Expected behavior: the update should make the corresponding regression test pass.")
+
+    return "\n".join(lines), "commit", None

+"""Problem statement synthesis helpers."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from collections.abc import Mapping
+from typing import Any
+
+
+def _first_string(*values: Any) -> str:
+    for value in values:
+        if isinstance(value, str):
+            candidate = value.strip()
+            if candidate:
+                return candidate
+    return ""
+
+
+def _nested_string(record: Mapping[str, Any], *keys: str) -> str:
+    value: Any = record
+    for key in keys:
+        if not isinstance(value, Mapping):
+            return ""
+        value = value.get(key)
+    return _first_string(value)
+
+
+def _nested_value(record: Mapping[str, Any], *keys: str) -> Any:
+    value: Any = record
+    for key in keys:
+        if not isinstance(value, Mapping):
+            return None
+        value = value.get(key)
+    return value
+
+
+def _issue_reference(record: Mapping[str, Any]) -> str:
+    refs = record.get("issue_refs")
+    if isinstance(refs, list):
+        for ref in refs:
+            if isinstance(ref, str) and ref.strip():
+                return ref.strip()
+            if isinstance(ref, (int, float)):
+                return str(ref)
+    return _first_string(
+        record.get("issue_ref"),
+        record.get("issue_id"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "issue_ref"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "issue_id"),
+    )
+
+
+def _file_names_from_patch(patch: str) -> list[str]:
+    names: list[str] = []
+    for line in patch.splitlines():
+        if not line.startswith("diff --git "):
+            continue
+        parts = line.split()
+        if len(parts) >= 4:
+            for candidate in parts[2:4]:
+                if candidate.startswith("a/") or candidate.startswith("b/"):
+                    candidate = candidate[2:]
+                if candidate not in names:
+                    names.append(candidate)
+    return names
+
+
+def _commit_style_statement(subject: str, body: str, patch: str) -> str:
+    file_names = _file_names_from_patch(patch)
+    details: list[str] = []
+    if subject:
+        details.append(subject.rstrip("."))
+    if body:
+        details.append(body.strip())
+    if file_names:
+        details.append(f"Affected files: {', '.join(file_names)}.")
+    details.append("Run tests impacted by this change.")
+    observed = " ".join(details)
+    return f"Observed behavior: {observed}"
+
+
+def _is_weak_commit_text(subject: str, body: str) -> bool:
+    text = f"{subject} {body}".strip().lower()
+    if not text:
+        return True
+    if len(text) < 12:
+        return True
+    weak_subjects = {
+        "fix",
+        "update",
+        "changes",
+        "change",
+        "misc",
+        "wip",
+        "temp",
+        "tweak",
+        "refactor",
+        "patch",
+    }
+    subject_norm = subject.strip().lower()
+    return subject_norm in weak_subjects or subject_norm in {"fix bug", "fixes"}
+
+
+def synthesize_problem_statement(record: Mapping[str, Any], patch: str) -> tuple[str, str, str]:
+    """Return ``(statement, source, source_ref)`` for a candidate record."""
+
+    issue_title = _first_string(
+        record.get("issue_title"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "issue_title"),
+    )
+    issue_body = _first_string(
+        record.get("issue_body"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "issue_body"),
+    )
+    if issue_title or issue_body:
+        parts = [part for part in [issue_title, issue_body] if part]
+        statement = ": ".join([parts[0], " ".join(parts[1:])]) if len(parts) > 1 else parts[0]
+        source_ref = _issue_reference(record)
+        return statement.strip(), "linked_issue", source_ref
+
+    pr_title = _first_string(
+        record.get("pr_title"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "pr_title"),
+    )
+    pr_body = _first_string(
+        record.get("pr_body"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "pr_body"),
+    )
+    if pr_title or pr_body:
+        parts = [part for part in [pr_title, pr_body] if part]
+        statement = ": ".join([parts[0], " ".join(parts[1:])]) if len(parts) > 1 else parts[0]
+        source_ref = _first_string(
+            record.get("pr_ref"),
+            record.get("pr_url"),
+            record.get("pr_number"),
+            _nested_value(record, "metadata", "pr_ref"),
+            _nested_value(record, "metadata", "pr_url"),
+            _nested_value(record, "metadata", "pr_number"),
+        )
+        return statement.strip(), "pull_request", source_ref
+
+    subject = _first_string(
+        record.get("source_subject"),
+        record.get("commit_subject"),
+        record.get("subject"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "source_subject"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "commit_subject"),
+    )
+    body = _first_string(
+        record.get("source_body"),
+        record.get("commit_body"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "source_body"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "commit_body"),
+    )
+
+    advisory = _nested_value(record, "metadata", "llm_advisory")
+    advisory_statement = ""
+    advisory_ref = ""
+    if isinstance(advisory, Mapping):
+        advisory_statement = _first_string(advisory.get("problem_statement"))
+    advisory_ref = _first_string(
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "llm_model", "model_name"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "llm_model"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "llm_advisory", "model_name"),
+    )
+
+    if advisory_statement and _is_weak_commit_text(subject, body):
+        return advisory_statement, "llm_advisory", advisory_ref
+
+    if not subject and not body:
+        subject = _first_string(
+            record.get("commit"),
+            _nested_value(record, "metadata", "source_commit"),
+        )
+
+    statement = _commit_style_statement(subject, body, patch)
+    source_ref = _first_string(
+        record.get("commit"),
+        record.get("source_commit"),
+        _nested_value(record, "metadata", "source_commit"),
+    )
+    return statement.strip(), "commit", source_ref

     return result.stdout
 
 
+def get_commit_message(path: str | Path, commit: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
+    """Return the subject and body for a commit."""
+    root = get_repo_root(path)
+    result = run_command(["git", "-C", str(root), "show", "-s", "--format=%s%n%b", commit])
+    if not result.success:
+        raise GitError(f"failed reading commit message for {commit}: {result.stderr.strip() or result.stdout}")
+    output = result.stdout.splitlines()
+    if not output:
+        return "", ""
+    subject = output[0].strip()
+    body = "\n".join(line.rstrip() for line in output[1:]).strip()
+    return subject, body
+
+
 def apply_patch_text(
     path: str | Path,
     patch: str,

+"""Deterministic problem-statement synthesis for dataset instances."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
+
+
+def _get_value(record: Dict[str, Any], key: str) -> Any:
+    if key in record:
+        return record[key]
+    metadata = record.get("metadata")
+    if isinstance(metadata, dict) and key in metadata:
+        return metadata[key]
+    return None
+
+
+def _get_subject(record: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[str]:
+    for key in ("source_subject", "commit_subject"):
+        val = _get_value(record, key)
+        if val is not None and str(val).strip():
+            return str(val).strip()
+    return None
+
+
+def _get_body(record: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[str]:
+    for key in ("source_body", "commit_body"):
+        val = _get_value(record, key)
+        if val is not None and str(val).strip():
+            return str(val).strip()
+    return None
+
+
+def _is_weak_commit(text: str) -> bool:
+    cleaned = text.strip().lower()
+    if len(cleaned) <= 8:
+        return True
+    words = cleaned.split()
+    if len(words) <= 1:
+        return True
+    weak_starters = {
+        "fix",
+        "update",
+        "refactor",
+        "bump",
+        "merge",
+        "chore",
+        "docs",
+        "style",
+        "test",
+        "wip",
+        "patch",
+        "init",
+        "add",
+        "remove",
+        "delete",
+        "clean",
+        "revert",
+        "temp",
+        "todo",
+        "hack",
+    }
+    if words[0] in weak_starters and len(words) <= 2:
+        return True
+    return False
+
+
+def synthesize_problem_statement(
+    record: Dict[str, Any],
+    patch: str,
+) -> Tuple[str, str, Optional[str]]:
+    """
+    Generate an issue-style problem statement with provenance.
+
+    Priority order:
+    1. linked issue title/body
+    2. PR title/body
+    3. commit message plus diff summary
+    4. LLM-generated issue-style restatement
+    """
+    # Priority 1: linked issue
+    issue_title = _get_value(record, "issue_title")
+    issue_body = _get_value(record, "issue_body")
+    issue_refs = _get_value(record, "issue_refs")
+
+    if issue_title:
+        parts: List[str] = [str(issue_title).strip()]
+        if issue_body:
+            parts.append(str(issue_body).strip())
+        statement = "\n".join(parts)
+        source_ref = issue_refs[0] if isinstance(issue_refs, list) and issue_refs else None
+        return statement, "linked_issue", source_ref
+
+    # Priority 2: pull request
+    pr_title = _get_value(record, "pr_title")
+    pr_body = _get_value(record, "pr_body")
+    if pr_title:
+        parts = [str(pr_title).strip()]
+        if pr_body:
+            parts.append(str(pr_body).strip())
+        statement = "\n".join(parts)
+        return statement, "pull_request", None
+
+    # Priority 3 & 4: commit or LLM fallback
+    source_subject = _get_subject(record)
+    source_body = _get_body(record)
+    llm_advisory = _get_value(record, "llm_advisory")
+    llm_model = _get_value(record, "llm_model")
+
+    commit_text = source_subject or ""
+    is_weak = _is_weak_commit(commit_text)
+
+    if is_weak and isinstance(llm_advisory, dict):
+        ps = llm_advisory.get("problem_statement")
+        if ps:
+            return str(ps).strip(), "llm_advisory", str(llm_model) if llm_model is not None else None
+
+    # Commit fallback synthesis
+    metadata = record.get("metadata", {}) or {}
+    total_changed_lines = metadata.get("total_changed_lines") if isinstance(metadata, dict) else None
+
+    parts = []
+    if commit_text:
+        parts.append("Observed behavior")
+        parts.append(f"- {commit_text}")
+        if source_body:
+            for line in source_body.splitlines():
+                line = line.strip()
+                if line:
+                    parts.append(f"- {line}")
+
+    if patch and patch.strip():
+        if parts:
+            parts.append("")
+        parts.append("Reproduction")
+        parts.append("- run tests impacted by this change")
+        if total_changed_lines and isinstance(total_changed_lines, int):
+            parts.append(f"  ({total_changed_lines} changed lines)")
+
+    statement = "\n".join(parts)
+    if not statement:
+        statement = "No problem description available."
+
+    return statement, "commit", None
diff --git a/repogauge/utils/git.py b/repogauge/utils/git.py
index b2b774f..8c6d048 100644
--- a/repogauge/utils/git.py
+++ b/repogauge/utils/git.py
@@ -133,6 +133,18 @@ def create_worktree(
     return WorktreeHandle(repo=repo, path=temp_path)
 
 
+def extract_commit_message(path: str | Path, commit: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
+    """Return (subject, body) for a commit."""
+    root = get_repo_root(path)
+    result = run_command(["git", "-C", str(root), "log", "-1", "--format=%s%x00%b", commit])
+    if not result.success:
+        raise GitError(f"failed extracting message for {commit}: {result.stderr.strip() or result.stdout}")
+    parts = result.stdout.split("\x00", 1)
+    subject = parts[0].strip()
+    body = parts[1].strip() if len(parts) > 1 else ""
+    return subject, body
+
+
 def remove_worktree(path: str | Path, worktree_path: str | Path) -> None:
     """Remove a worktree and best-effort clean directory."""
     root = get_repo_root(path)

+def _to_test_label(commands: list[str]) -> str:
+    if not commands:
+        return "testunknown"
+    return "+".join(commands)
+
+
+def _to_pkg_label(managers: list[str]) -> str:
+    if not managers:
+        return "pkgunknown"
+    return "+".join(managers)
+
+
+def _to_python_label(versions: list[str]) -> str:
+    if not versions:
+        return "pyunknown"
+    return "_".join(f"py{v.replace('.', '')}" for v in versions)
+
+
+def _normalize_dependency_lines(raw: str) -> list[str]:
+    lines: list[str] = []
+    for raw_line in raw.splitlines():
+        value = raw_line.strip()
+        if not value or value.startswith("#"):
+            continue
+        value = value.split("#", 1)[0].strip()
+        if value:
+            lines.append(value)
+    return lines
+
+
+def _read_requirements_signature(repo_root: Path, profile: dict[str, Any]) -> list[str]:
+    if not repo_root.exists():
+        if isinstance(profile.get("package_style"), str):
+            return _sorted_unique([str(profile.get("package_style"))])
+        return []
+
+    requirements: list[str] = []
+    for candidate in sorted(
+        (
+            repo_root / "requirements.txt",
+            repo_root / "requirements-dev.txt",
+            repo_root / "dev-requirements.txt",
+        )
+    ):
+        if not candidate.exists():
+            continue
+        try:
+            normalized_lines = _normalize_dependency_lines(
+                candidate.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
+            )
+            requirements.append("\n".join(_sorted_unique(normalized_lines)))
+        except OSError:
+            requirements.append("")
+    pyproject = repo_root / "pyproject.toml"
+    if pyproject.exists():
+        try:
+            normalized_lines = _normalize_dependency_lines(
+                pyproject.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
+            )
+            requirements.append("\n".join(_sorted_unique(normalized_lines)))
+        except OSError:
+            requirements.append("")
+    setup_cfg = repo_root / "setup.cfg"
+    if setup_cfg.exists():
+        try:
+            normalized_lines = _normalize_dependency_lines(
+                setup_cfg.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
+            )
+            requirements.append("\n".join(_sorted_unique(normalized_lines)))
+        except OSError:
+            requirements.append("")
+    setup_py = repo_root / "setup.py"
+    if setup_py.exists():
+        try:
+            normalized_lines = _normalize_dependency_lines(
+                setup_py.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
+            )
+            requirements.append("\n".join(_sorted_unique(normalized_lines)))
+        except OSError:
+            requirements.append("")
+    if not requirements and isinstance(profile.get("package_style"), str):
+        requirements.append(profile["package_style"])
+    return _sorted_unique(requirements)
+

diff --git a/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
new file mode 100644

+++ b/repogauge.egg-info/PKG-INFO
@@ -0,0 +1,54 @@
+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.

+
+_CONFIG_BUILD_DIRS = {
+    ".github", ".circleci", ".travis", ".gitlab", ".azure-pipelines",
+}
+
+_CONFIG_BUILD_EXTENSIONS = {".cfg", ".ini", ".toml", ".yml", ".yaml"}
+
+_DOCS_DIRS = {"docs", "doc", "documentation"}
+
+_DOCS_EXTENSIONS = {".md", ".rst", ".txt", ".adoc", ".asciidoc"}
+
+_RUNTIME_EXTENSIONS = {
+    ".py", ".js", ".ts", ".jsx", ".tsx", ".go", ".rb", ".java",
+    ".kt", ".scala", ".rs", ".c", ".cpp", ".cc", ".h", ".hpp",
+    ".cs", ".swift", ".php", ".sh", ".bash", ".zsh",
+}
+
+
+@dataclass
+class FileRole:
+    role: str
+    reason: str
+
+
+def classify_file(path: str) -> FileRole:
+    """Classify a file path into a role category."""
+    p = PurePosixPath(path)
+    parts = p.parts
+    name = p.name
+    suffix = p.suffix.lower()
+
+    # Check vendor/generated directories first (highest priority for exclusion)
+    for part in parts[:-1]:
+        if part in _VENDOR_GENERATED_DIRS or part.startswith(".venv"):
+            return FileRole("generated_vendor", "vendor or generated build cache directory")
+
+    # Check test files (files named test_*.py or *_test.py)
+    if name.startswith("test_") and suffix == ".py":
+        return FileRole("test", "test filename convention")
+    if name.endswith("_test.py"):
+        return FileRole("test", "test filename convention")
+
+    # Check test support (non-test files under a tests/ directory)
+    if parts and parts[0] in {"tests", "test", "spec"}:
+        return FileRole("test_support", "test-support path under tests")
+
+    # Check docs
+    if parts and parts[0] in _DOCS_DIRS:
+        return FileRole("docs", "documentation file or directory")
+    if suffix in _DOCS_EXTENSIONS:
+        return FileRole("docs", "documentation file or directory")
+
+    # Check config/build files
+    if parts and parts[0] in _CONFIG_BUILD_DIRS:
+        return FileRole("config_build", "CI, package, or tooling configuration file")
+    if name in _CONFIG_BUILD_NAMES:
+        return FileRole("config_build", "CI, package, or tooling configuration file")
+    if suffix in _CONFIG_BUILD_EXTENSIONS:
+        return FileRole("config_build", "CI, package, or tooling configuration file")
+
+    # Check prod (runtime source files)
+    if suffix in _RUNTIME_EXTENSIONS:
+        return FileRole("prod", "runtime source extension")
+
+    return FileRole("unknown", "No explicit role rule matched")

diff --git a/repogauge/mining/file_roles.py b/repogauge/mining/file_roles.py
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..6456cc3
--- /dev/null
+++ b/repogauge/mining/file_roles.py
@@ -0,0 +1,175 @@
+"""Canonical file-role classification for RepoGauge."""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass
+from pathlib import Path, PurePosixPath
+
+FILE_ROLES = (
+    "prod",
+    "test",
+    "test_support",
+    "config_build",
+    "docs",
+    "generated_vendor",
+    "unknown",
+)
+
+_TEST_DIR_NAMES = {"tests", "test"}
+_DOC_DIR_NAMES = {"docs", "doc"}
+_VENDOR_DIR_NAMES = {
+    ".venv",
+    "venv",
+    ".tox",
+    ".nox",
+    "node_modules",
+    "site-packages",
+    "dist-packages",
+    "__pycache__",
+    "vendor",
+    "third_party",
+    "third-party",
+    "build",
+    "dist",
+    "target",
+}
+_CONFIG_FILENAMES = {
+    "makefile",
+    "dockerfile",
+    "pyproject.toml",
+    "setup.py",
+    "setup.cfg",
+    "tox.ini",
+    "noxfile.py",
+    "pytest.ini",
+    "requirements.txt",
+}
+_CONFIG_PREFIXES = ("requirements",)
+_DOC_FILENAMES = {
+    "readme",
+    "readme.md",
+    "readme.rst",
+    "changelog",
+    "changelog.md",
+    "changelog.rst",
+    "license",
+    "license.md",
+    "license.rst",
+    "contributing",
+    "contributing.md",
+    "contributing.rst",
+}
+
+
+@dataclass(frozen=True)
+class FileRoleClassification:
+    role: str
+    reason: str
+
+
+def _normalise_path(path: str | Path) -> PurePosixPath:
+    text = str(path).replace("\\", "/")
+    return PurePosixPath(text)
+
+
+def _basename(path: PurePosixPath) -> str:
+    return path.name.lower()
+
+
+def _parts_lower(path: PurePosixPath) -> list[str]:
+    return [part.lower() for part in path.parts if part not in ("", ".")]
+
+
+def _has_vendor_marker(parts: list[str]) -> bool:
+    return any(part in _VENDOR_DIR_NAMES for part in parts)
+
+
+def _has_doc_marker(parts: list[str], basename: str) -> bool:
+    return any(part in _DOC_DIR_NAMES for part in parts) or basename in _DOC_FILENAMES
+
+
+def _has_config_marker(parts: list[str], basename: str) -> bool:
+    if basename in _CONFIG_FILENAMES:
+        return True
+    if any(part == ".github" for part in parts) and "workflows" in parts:
+        return True
+    if basename.startswith(_CONFIG_PREFIXES):
+        return True
+    if basename.endswith((".yml", ".yaml", ".toml", ".ini", ".cfg", ".json", ".txt")):
+        return basename in {
+            "pyproject.toml",
+            "setup.cfg",
+            "tox.ini",
+            "noxfile.py",
+            "pytest.ini",
+            "requirements.txt",
+        } or basename.startswith("requirements")
+    return False
+
+
+def _has_test_marker(parts: list[str], basename: str) -> bool:
+    if "tests" in parts or "test" in parts:
+        if basename.startswith("test_") or basename.endswith("_test.py") or basename.endswith(".test.py"):
+            return True
+    return basename.startswith("test_") or basename.endswith("_test.py") or basename.endswith(".test.py")
+
+
+def _has_test_support_marker(parts: list[str], basename: str) -> bool:
+    if not any(part in _TEST_DIR_NAMES for part in parts):
+        return False
+    if _has_test_marker(parts, basename):
+        return False
+    return True
+
+
+def classify_file(path: str | Path) -> FileRoleClassification:
+    """Classify a file path into the RepoGauge file-role taxonomy."""
+
+    normalized = _normalise_path(path)
+    parts = _parts_lower(normalized)
+    basename = _basename(normalized)
+
+    if _has_vendor_marker(parts):
+        return FileRoleClassification(
+            role="generated_vendor",
+            reason="Matched vendor or generated build cache directory",
+        )
+
+    if _has_test_marker(parts, basename):
+        return FileRoleClassification(
+            role="test",
+            reason="Matched test filename convention",
+        )
+
+    if _has_test_support_marker(parts, basename):
+        return FileRoleClassification(
+            role="test_support",
+            reason="Matched test-support path under tests",
+        )
+
+    if _has_config_marker(parts, basename):
+        return FileRoleClassification(
+            role="config_build",
+            reason="Matched CI, package, or tooling configuration file",
+        )
+
+    if _has_doc_marker(parts, basename):
+        return FileRoleClassification(
+            role="docs",
+            reason="Matched documentation file or directory",
+        )
+
+    suffix = normalized.suffix.lower()
+    if suffix == ".py":
+        return FileRoleClassification(
+            role="prod",
+            reason="Matched runtime source extension",
+        )
+
+    return FileRoleClassification(
+        role="unknown",
+        reason="No explicit role rule matched",
+    )
+
+
+__all__ = ["FILE_ROLES", "FileRoleClassification", "classify_file"]

+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.

+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

Confidence

Candidate fixes the core classname splitting behavior in production, but it omits the regression test added by the gold patch and introduces substantial unrelated packaging churn.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

The production change addresses the reported JUnit classname issue and matches the intended split-at-first-PascalCase approach, so the main bug is fixed. However, unlike the gold patch, it does not add the targeted regression test that demonstrates the expected three-part pytest node ID behavior.

Correctness Safetysame Δ+0

The candidate implementation is semantically equivalent to the gold fix for the core behavior: it separates module path from class components at the first uppercase segment and constructs canonical IDs correctly for module-only and class-based cases. I do not see an obvious regression relative to gold in the production logic shown.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The implementation is reasonably clear, but it is slightly less polished than gold: the helper naming and docstring are narrower, and returning a list of class parts instead of a joined class chain makes the abstraction a bit less cohesive. The added egg-info files also add repository noise that hurts long-term maintainability.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

The gold patch adds a focused regression test covering both class-based and standalone test IDs. The candidate adds no corresponding test coverage, so the fix is left unguarded against future regressions.

Change Focusmuch worse Δ-2

The candidate includes multiple unrelated generated `repogauge.egg-info/*` files that have nothing to do with the JUnit parser bugfix. The gold patch stays tightly scoped to the production file and its regression test.

+Metadata-Version: 2.4
+Name: repogauge
+Version: 0.0.0
+Summary: Local SWE-bench-style dataset and harness helper for repositories
+Requires-Python: >=3.10
+Description-Content-Type: text/markdown
+
+# repogauge
+
+## v1 Scope and non-goals
+
+RepoGauge v1 is a **Python-only, local-first CLI** for creating local SWE-bench-style
+evaluation tasks from a repository and evaluating patches with the official SWE-bench harness.
+
+What v1 is:
+
+- Mine and shortlist candidate bugfix commits with deterministic heuristics.
+- Export SWE-bench-compatible `dataset.jsonl` artifacts.
+- Generate a repository-specific harness adapter so official evaluation can run
+  against previously unsupported repos.
+- Validate gold patches and `FAIL_TO_PASS` / `PASS_TO_PASS` outcomes deterministically.
+
+What v1 is not:
+
+- Multi-language generality.
+- Multi-commit PR reconstruction.
+- Synthetic test generation.
+- Hosted service or database-backed workflow orchestration.
+- Remote model calls by default.
+
+See the architecture docs:
+
+- [docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md](docs/ADRs/0001-mvp-architecture.md)
+- [DESIGN.md](DESIGN.md)
+
+## CLI surface (scaffold)
+
+- `repogauge mine PATH --out DIR`
+- `repogauge review CANDIDATES --out DIR`
+- `repogauge export REVIEWED --dataset DIR`
+- `repogauge eval DATASET --gold`
+- `repogauge run MATRIX`
+- `repogauge analyze RUN`
+- `repogauge train-router RUN`
+
+Global behavior:
+
+- `--config`: merges config files over built-in defaults.
+- `--out`: sets output directory root.
+- `--resume`: continues from existing outputs where possible.
+- `--dry-run`: validates parameters without writing artifacts.
+- `--llm-mode`: `off`, `local_only`, or `allow_remote`.
+
+### In scope for MVP
+
+- CLI-only workflows such as:
+  - `repogauge mine /path/to/repo --out ./out`
+  - `repogauge review ./out/candidates.jsonl`
+  - `repogauge export ./out/reviewed.jsonl --dataset ./out/dataset`
+  - `repogauge eval ./out/dataset/dataset.jsonl --gold`
+- Mining candidate bugfix commits from the default branch or an explicit commit range.
+- Materializing SWE-bench-style instances with:
+  - `instance_id`
+  - `repo`
+  - `base_commit`
+  - `problem_statement`
+  - `version`
+  - `patch`
+  - `test_patch`
+  - `FAIL_TO_PASS`
+  - `PASS_TO_PASS`
+  - optional metadata
+- Generating a repo-specific adapter that patches the official harness runtime maps.
+- Validating gold patches locally and through the official harness.
+- Running experiment matrices across multiple solver adapters and evaluating them through the judge path.
+- Producing per-run cost/quality reports and router-training data.
+
+Current release state is scaffolded and in active development.
+
+## Running repogauge against itself
+
+```bash
+scripts/gauge_self.sh
+```
+
+Options:
+
+| Flag | Default | Description |
+|---|---|---|
+| `--out DIR` | `./out` | Root directory for all artifacts |
+| `--max-commits N` | `100` | Commits to scan |
+| `--decisions FILE` | _(none)_ | JSONL file of manual accept/reject decisions |
+
+Outputs written under `--out`:
+
+```
+mine/repo_profile.json              repo identity and environment hints
+mine/candidates.jsonl               all scanned commits with heuristic scores
+review/reviewed.jsonl               accept/reject decisions
+review/review.html                  human-readable review report
+export/dataset/dataset.jsonl        SWE-bench-compatible instances
+export/dataset/predictions.gold.jsonl
+```
+
+### E2E integration test
+
+```bash
+uv run python -m pytest tests/e2e/test_self_gauge.py -v
+```
+
+This runs the full mine → review → export pipeline against this repository and
+validates every artifact at each stage.

     """Raised when the JUnit XML cannot be parsed."""
 
 
+def _split_classname(classname: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
+    """Split a pytest classname into module path and optional class chain.
+
+    Pytest reports class-based tests as ``module.path.ClassName`` in the JUnit
+    ``classname`` field.  The first PascalCase component marks the start of the
+    class chain; everything before it is the filesystem path.
+    """
+    parts = classname.split(".")
+    split_index = None
+    for index, part in enumerate(parts):
+        if part and part[0].isupper():
+            split_index = index
+            break
+
+    if split_index is None:
+        return classname, ""
+
+    module_part = ".".join(parts[:split_index])
+    class_part = ".".join(parts[split_index:])
+    return module_part, class_part
+
+
 def _classname_to_path(classname: str) -> str:
     """Convert ``tests.unit.test_foo`` → ``tests/unit/test_foo.py``."""
-    parts = classname.split(".")
-    # Heuristic: if any component starts with "test_" or equals "tests",
-    # assume it is a file/directory component and convert dots to slashes.
-    return "/".join(parts) + ".py"
+    module_part, _ = _split_classname(classname)
+    if not module_part:
+        return ""
+    return "/".join(module_part.split(".")) + ".py"
 
 
 def _canonical_id(classname: str, name: str) -> str:
@@ -43,9 +65,17 @@ def _canonical_id(classname: str, name: str) -> str:
 
     pytest encodes parametrized cases as ``name[param]``; we preserve that as-is.
     """
-    path_part = _classname_to_path(classname) if classname else ""
+    if not classname:
+        return name
+
+    module_part, class_part = _split_classname(classname)
+    path_part = _classname_to_path(classname)
+    if path_part and class_part:
+        return f"{path_part}::{class_part.replace('.', '::')}::{name}"
     if path_part:
         return f"{path_part}::{name}"
+    if class_part:
+        return f"{class_part.replace('.', '::')}::{name}"
     return name

+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import hashlib
+import json
+import re
+from pathlib import Path
+from typing import Any
+
+try:
+    import tomllib
+except ModuleNotFoundError:  # pragma: no cover - Python < 3.11 fallback
+    tomllib = None  # type: ignore[assignment]
+
+
+REPO_VERSION_UNKNOWN = "repover_unknown"
+
+
+def _as_sorted_unique(values: list[str]) -> list[str]:
+    return sorted(set(values))
+
+
+def _safe_read_text(path: Path) -> str:
+    try:
+        return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
+    except OSError:
+        return ""
+
+
+def _normalize_python_versions(values: Any) -> list[str]:
+    normalized: list[str] = []
+    for value in values or []:
+        match = re.search(r"\b3\.(\d+)\b", str(value))
+        if match:
+            normalized.append(f"3.{match.group(1)}")
+    return _as_sorted_unique(normalized)
+
+
+def _normalize_tokens(values: Any) -> list[str]:
+    return _as_sorted_unique([str(value).strip() for value in values or [] if str(value).strip()])
+
+
+def _normalize_requirement_line(line: str) -> str:
+    stripped = line.strip()
+    if not stripped or stripped.startswith("#"):
+        return ""
+    if " #" in stripped:
+        stripped = stripped.split(" #", 1)[0].rstrip()
+    stripped = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", stripped)
+    return stripped
+
+
+def _normalize_requirements_text(raw: str) -> list[str]:
+    normalized = [_normalize_requirement_line(line) for line in raw.splitlines()]
+    return _as_sorted_unique([line for line in normalized if line])
+
+
+def _extract_pyproject_dependency_lines(pyproject_path: Path) -> list[str]:
+    if tomllib is None:
+        return _normalize_requirements_text(_safe_read_text(pyproject_path))
+
+    try:
+        data = tomllib.loads(_safe_read_text(pyproject_path))
+    except Exception:
+        return _normalize_requirements_text(_safe_read_text(pyproject_path))
+
+    lines: list[str] = []
+
+    project = data.get("project", {})
+    for dep in project.get("dependencies", []) or []:
+        lines.append(str(dep).strip())
+    for extra_name, deps in (project.get("optional-dependencies", {}) or {}).items():
+        for dep in deps or []:
+            lines.append(f"{extra_name}:{str(dep).strip()}")
+
+    poetry = data.get("tool", {}).get("poetry", {})
+    for dep_name, dep_value in (poetry.get("dependencies", {}) or {}).items():
+        if dep_name.lower() == "python":
+            continue
+        if isinstance(dep_value, str):
+            lines.append(f"{dep_name}{dep_value.strip()}")
+        elif isinstance(dep_value, dict):
+            lines.append(f"{dep_name}:{json.dumps(dep_value, sort_keys=True)}")
+        else:
+            lines.append(f"{dep_name}:{dep_value}")
+    for dep_name, dep_value in (poetry.get("dev-dependencies", {}) or {}).items():
+        if isinstance(dep_value, str):
+            lines.append(f"dev:{dep_name}{dep_value.strip()}")
+        elif isinstance(dep_value, dict):
+            lines.append(f"dev:{dep_name}:{json.dumps(dep_value, sort_keys=True)}")
+        else:
+            lines.append(f"dev:{dep_name}:{dep_value}")
+
+    return _as_sorted_unique([line for line in lines if line])
+
+
+def _detect_repo_version(profile: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
+    repo_version = str(profile.get("repo_version") or "").strip()
+    if repo_version:
+        return repo_version
+
+    repo_root = Path(profile["repo_root"])
+    pyproject_path = repo_root / "pyproject.toml"
+    if pyproject_path.exists():
+        if tomllib is not None:
+            try:
+                data = tomllib.loads(_safe_read_text(pyproject_path))
+            except Exception:
+                data = {}
+            project = data.get("project", {})
+            version = str(project.get("version") or "").strip()
+            if version:
+                return version
+            poetry = data.get("tool", {}).get("poetry", {})
+            version = str(poetry.get("version") or "").strip()
+            if version:
+                return version
+        text = _safe_read_text(pyproject_path)
+        for pattern in (
+            r'(?m)^\s*version\s*=\s*"([^"]+)"\s*$',
+            r"(?m)^\s*version\s*=\s*'([^']+)'\s*$",
+        ):
+            match = re.search(pattern, text)
+            if match:
+                return match.group(1).strip()
+
+    return REPO_VERSION_UNKNOWN
+
+
+def _dependency_inputs(profile: dict[str, Any]) -> list[str]:
+    repo_root = Path(profile["repo_root"])
+    inputs: list[str] = []
+
+    requirements_files = sorted(repo_root.glob("requirements*.txt"))
+    for req_file in requirements_files:
+        inputs.extend(_normalize_requirements_text(_safe_read_text(req_file)))
+
+    pyproject_path = repo_root / "pyproject.toml"
+    if pyproject_path.exists():
+        inputs.extend(_extract_pyproject_dependency_lines(pyproject_path))
+
+    pipfile_path = repo_root / "Pipfile"
+    if pipfile_path.exists():
+        inputs.extend(_normalize_requirements_text(_safe_read_text(pipfile_path)))
+
+    uv_lock_path = repo_root / "uv.lock"
+    if uv_lock_path.exists():
+        inputs.extend(_normalize_requirements_text(_safe_read_text(uv_lock_path)))
+
+    return _as_sorted_unique(inputs)
+
+
+def _build_dependency_signature(inputs: list[str]) -> str:
+    payload = json.dumps(inputs, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":"))
+    return hashlib.sha256(payload.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
+
+
+def build_environment_signature(profile: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
+    repo_version = _detect_repo_version(profile)
+    python_hints = profile.get("python_hints", {}) or {}
+    test_runner_hints = profile.get("test_runner_hints", {}) or {}
+    python_versions = _normalize_python_versions(python_hints.get("versions", []))
+    test_commands = _normalize_tokens(test_runner_hints.get("commands", []))
+    package_managers = _normalize_tokens(python_hints.get("package_managers", []))
+    dependency_inputs = _dependency_inputs(profile)
+    dependency_signature = _build_dependency_signature(dependency_inputs)
+
+    py_segment = "_".join(f"py{v.replace('.', '')}" for v in python_versions) if python_versions else "pyunknown"
+    test_segment = "+".join(test_commands) if test_commands else "unknown"
+    package_segment = "+".join(package_managers) if package_managers else "unknown"
+    version = f"{repo_version}__{py_segment}__{test_segment}__{package_segment}__reqhash_{dependency_signature}"
+
+    return {
+        "repo_version": repo_version,
+        "python_versions": python_versions,
+        "test_runner_commands": test_commands,
+        "package_managers": package_managers,
+        "dependency_inputs": dependency_inputs,
+        "dependency_signature": dependency_signature,
+        "version": version,
+        "signature": version,
+    }

Candidate mostly implements environment signature generation, but it diverges from the gold fix in important ways: repo version detection is incomplete, the signature schema/fallback labels differ, and it omits the regression tests that anchor the intended behavior.

Task Fitworse Δ-1

It adds environment signature support and populates `repo_version`/`version`, but it does not match the full task coverage of the gold patch. In particular, repo version detection only handles `pyproject.toml` and misses the gold fix’s `setup.cfg` and `setup.py` paths, which were part of the required deterministic version key behavior.

Correctness Safetyworse Δ-1

The candidate introduces behavioral gaps and format drift versus gold. `_detect_repo_version()` ignores `setup.cfg` and `setup.py`, so some repositories will incorrectly stay at `repover_unknown`. It also changes fallback label semantics from `testunknown`/`pkgunknown` to plain `unknown`, which alters signature stability and compatibility relative to the intended format. The adapter-coupled implementation is also riskier than the gold patch’s self-contained helper for this targeted change.

Maintainabilityworse Δ-1

The gold patch keeps version extraction in `inspect.py` and signature construction in a straightforward helper. The candidate makes `build_environment_signature()` more coupled to adapter lookup and profile shape, adds extra fields not needed for the task, and broadens the logic beyond the stated fix. That makes the implementation harder to reason about for a regression-focused change.

Test Qualitymuch worse Δ-2

The gold patch adds focused unit coverage in both `tests/unit/test_inspect.py` and `tests/unit/test_signature.py` for repo-version extraction, deterministic signatures, fallback behavior, and normalization. The candidate patch includes no test changes at all, so it does not demonstrate or lock in the regression fix.

Change Focusworse Δ-1

The candidate stays in the general area of the bug, but it adds unrelated API surface in `repogauge/mining/__init__.py` and broadens the implementation toward adapter-driven generalization instead of the narrower repository-version/signature fix in the gold patch.
